                    <script type="text/javascript">
                    function RadWindowprompt_detectenter(id, ev, input)
                    {
                        if (!ev) ev = window.event;
                        if (ev.keyCode == 13)
                        {
                            var but = input.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("A")[0];
                            if (but)
                            {
                                if (but.click) but.click();
                                else if (but.onclick)
                                {
                                    but.focus(); var click = but.onclick; but.onclick = null; if (click) click.call(but);
                                }
                            }
                           return false;
                        }
                        else return true;
                    }
                    </script>
                    <input title="Enter Value" onkeydown="return RadWindowprompt_detectenter('{0}', event, this);" type="text" class="rwDialogInput" value="{2}">

    <script type="text/javascript">

        function OnClientFocusHandler(sender, eventArgs) {
            if (!sender.get_dropDownVisible()) {
                sender.showDropDown();
            }
        }

        function OnLossItemsRequesting(sender, args) {
            args.get_context()["Values"] = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_LossType").get_value();
        }

        function OnClientDropDownClosed(sender) {

            if ((sender.get_id() == $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_LossType").get_id())) {
                $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_SecondryLossType").clearSelection();
                $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_SecondryLossType").clearItems();
            }
        }

        function SearchLosstype(sender, eventArgs) {

            var hddService = document.getElementById('ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_hddService');
            if (sender.get_id() == $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_SecondryLossType").get_id()) {
                var secLossId = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_SecondryLossType").get_value();
                hddService.value = 'ddlSecondryLossType';
                ProductService.SetLossType(secLossId, OnWSRequestCompleteLoss, OnWSRequestFailedLoss);
            }
        }

        function OnWSRequestCompleteLoss(results) {
            var hddService = document.getElementById('ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_hddService');
            var splits = results.split(",");

            if (results != null && results != "") {
                if (hddService.value == 'ddlSecondryLossType') {
                    $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_LossType").set_text(splits[1]);
                    $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_comboBox_LossType").set_value(splits[0]);
                }
            }
        }

        function OnWSRequestFailedLoss(error) {
            alert("Error in Calling Method.");
        }

        function ValidateLossDate(sender, args) {
            var dates = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_DatePicker_DateOffLoss");
            alert('Enter valid date of loss.');
            args.set_cancel(true);
            sender.clear();
        }

        function updateCalendarFooter() {
            var today = new Date();
            var days = ["Sunday", "Monday", "Tuesday", "Wednesday", "Thursday", "Friday", "Saturday"];
            var months = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June", "July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"];

            var dayName = days[today.getDay()];
            var monthName = months[today.getMonth()];
            var day = today.getDate();
            var year = today.getFullYear();

            var formattedDate = dayName + ", " + monthName + " " + day + ", " + year;

            var footerDiv = document.getElementById("calendarFooterDiv");
            if (footerDiv) {
                footerDiv.innerText = formattedDate;
                footerDiv.style.backgroundColor = "#c3d8f1";
                footerDiv.style.padding = "5px";
            }

            var footerDiv = document.getElementById("calendarFooterDiv");
            if (footerDiv) {
                footerDiv.innerText = formattedDate;
            }
        }

        $telerik.$(function () {
            var datePicker = $find("ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_GenaralInfo_DatePicker_DateOffLoss");
             if (datePicker) {
                 datePicker.add_popupOpening(function () {
                     updateCalendarFooter();
                 });
             }
         });

    </script>

#calendarFooterDiv {
    text-align: center;
    padding-top: 5px;
}

            <td style="width: 98%; padding-top: 12px; padding-left: 8px; padding-bottom: 10px;" class="DashShadowBox">
                <span class="DashTitle" style="padding-left: 3px;">
                    <span id="ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_LabelInternalParticipants">Internal Participants</span>
                </span>

                
    <script type="text/javascript">

        function OnClientFocusHandlerParticipants(sender, eventArgs) {
            if (!sender.get_dropDownVisible()) {
                sender.showDropDown();
            }
        }

        function OnClientFocusHandler(sender, eventArgs) {
            if (!sender.get_dropDownVisible()) {
                sender.showDropDown();
            }
        }

        function EstimatorComboBoxSelectedIndexChanged(sender, eventArgs) {
            var selectedEmployeeID = sender.get_selectedItem().get_value();
            var selectedElementId = sender.get_id();

            var onCompensationPlanForUserRequestComplete = function (results, args) {
                var combobox = $find(selectedElementId.replace("EstimatorComboBox", "CompensationPlanComboBox"));

                if (results === "") {
                    combobox.clearSelection();
                }
                else {
                    var splits = results.split(",")

                    if (splits[1] == "") {
                        combobox.clearSelection();
                    }
                    else {
                        combobox.set_text(splits[0]);
                        combobox.set_value(splits[1]);
                    }
                }
            };

            var onCompensationPlanForUserRequestFailed = function (error) {
                alert("Getting error during Get Compensation Plan For User.");
            };

            if (selectedEmployeeID != null) {
                NextGear.Dash.Services.Shared.CreateClaim.DropDownsService.GetCompensationPlanForUser(
                    selectedEmployeeID, onCompensationPlanForUserRequestComplete, onCompensationPlanForUserRequestFailed);
            }
        }
    </script>

            <td id="ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_tdPolicy" style="width: 98.5%; padding-top: 12px; padding-left: 0px; padding-bottom: 10px;" class="DashShadowBox">

                    <span id="ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_InsuranceInformationLabel">External Participants</span></span>
                
<script>
    var primaryMortgageTypeID = 14;
    function SearchCustomCompanyName(sender, args) {

        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";

        var controlName = document.getElementById(placeHolder+"ControlNameHidden");
        var externalParticipant = document.getElementById(sender.get_id());

        var childContact = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-childControlID');
        var parentCompany = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ParentControlID');
        var ContactId = $find(sender.get_id()).get_value();
        var externalParticipantTypeID = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-systemid');

        if (parentCompany != null) {
            controlName.value = placeHolder + parentCompany;
            NextGear.Dash.Services.Shared.CreateClaim.DropDownsService.SetCompanyDropDown(ContactId, OnWSCustomRequestComplete, OnCompanyRequestFailed);
        }

        if (externalParticipantTypeID == primaryMortgageTypeID &&
            checkIsNull(externalParticipant.control._text) == false) {
            manageCoreLogicLogo(externalParticipant.control._value);
        }
    }

    function ClearCustomParticipantCombobox(sender, args) {
        var externalParticipant = document.getElementById(sender.get_id());

        var childContact = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-childControlID')
        var externalParticipantType = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ExternalParticipantType').split(",");
        var externalParticipantTypeID = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ExternalParticipantTypeid');

        if (childContact != null) {
            childContact.split(",").forEach(ClearDropDownLists);
        }

        if (externalParticipantTypeID == primaryMortgageTypeID &&
            checkIsNull(externalParticipant.control._text)) {
            hideLogo("coreLogicLogo");
        }
    }

    function ClearDropDownLists(contactDropDown, index) {

        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";

        var DropDown = $find(placeHolder + contactDropDown);

        DropDown.clearSelection();
        DropDown.clearItems();
    }

    function OnWSCustomRequestComplete(results) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = document.getElementById(placeHolder + "ControlNameHidden").value;
        var combobox = $find(controlName);
        var splits = results.split(",");
        combobox.set_text(splits[1]);
        combobox.set_value(splits[0]);
    }

    function OnCompanyRequestFailed(error) {
        alert("No employees are there for this company");
    }

    function OnClientFocusHandlerForCustomParticipant(sender, eventArgs) {
        if (!sender.get_dropDownVisible()) {
            sender.showDropDown();
        }
    }

    function OnExternalParticipantClientRequesting(sender, args) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";

        var externalParticipant = document.getElementById(sender.get_id());
        var parentID = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ParentControlID');

        if (parentID != null) {
            args.get_context()["Values"] = $find(placeHolder + parentID).get_value();
            args.get_context()["HasParent"] = true;
        }
        else {
            args.get_context()["Values"] = null;
            args.get_context()["HasParent"] = false;
        }

        args.get_context()["ExternalParticipantTypeID"] = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ExternalParticipantTypeID');
        args.get_context()["ExternalParticipantType"] = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-ExternalParticipantType');
        args.get_context()["ExternalParticipantID"] = externalParticipant.getAttribute('data-SystemID');
    }

    function RebindIndividual(controlID, ID, Name) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var combobox = $find(placeHolder + controlID);
            combobox.set_text(Name);
            combobox.set_value(ID);
    }

    function RebindCompany(controlID, ID, Name) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";

        var combobox = $find(placeHolder + controlID);
            combobox.set_text(Name);
            combobox.set_value(ID);

        if (controlID == 'SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_14') {
            manageCoreLogicLogo(ID);
        }
    }

    function RebindBillToContact(controlID, ID, Name, BillToType) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var billToType = document.getElementById(placeHolder + "Hidden_BillToContactType");
            billToType.value = BillToType;
        var combobox = $find(placeHolder + controlID);
            combobox.set_text(Name);
            combobox.set_value(ID + ':' + BillToType);
    }

    function OnSelectedIndexChanged_BillToCompany(sender, args) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = placeHolder + "SystemIndividualParticipantCombobox_35";
        var combo = $find(controlName);
            combo.clearSelection();
            combo.clearItems();
    }

    function OnTextChange_BillToCompany(sender, args) {
        if(sender.get_text().length == 0) {
            SetDefaultValue_BillToContact();
        }
    }

    function OnItemRequesting_BillToContact(sender, args) {
        var serachText = args.get_text();
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = placeHolder + "SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_26";        
        var combo = $find(controlName);
        var context = args.get_context();
            context["billToCompanyID"] = combo.get_value();
    }

    function OnSelectedIndexChanged_BillToContact(sender, args) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = placeHolder + "SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_26";
        var combo = $find(controlName);
        var contactID = sender.get_value();

        if(contactID == '0:0')
        {
            combo.clearSelection();
            combo.clearItems();
        }
        else if(contactID != '') 
        { 
           contactID = contactID.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');          
           NextGear.Dash.Services.Shared.CreateClaim.DropDownsService.SetCompanyDropDown(contactID, SetBillToCompanyField, ClearBillToCompanyField);
        }
    }

    function SetBillToCompanyField(results) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = placeHolder + "SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_26";
        var combobox = $find(controlName);

        if(results)
        {
            var splits = results.split(",");
            combobox.set_text(splits[1]);
            combobox.set_value(splits[0]);
        }
    }
    function ClearBillToCompanyField() {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlNameBillToCompany = placeHolder + "SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_26";
        var combobox = $find(controlNameBillToCompany);

        if (combobox) {
            combobox.clearSelection();
            combobox.clearItems();
        }
    }

    function SetBillToCompanyFieldAsCustomer(isCompanyCustomer) {
       var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
       var controlNameBillToCompany = placeHolder + "SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_26";
       var combobox = $find(controlNameBillToCompany);

       if(combobox)
       {
            combobox.clearSelection();
            combobox.clearItems();

            if(isCompanyCustomer)
            {
              var comboboxItem = new Telerik.Web.UI.RadComboBoxItem();                 
                  comboboxItem.set_text("Same As Company Customer");
                  combobox.get_items().add(comboboxItem);
                  combobox.get_items().getItem(0).select();
            }
            else
            {
                SetDefaultValue_BillToContact();
            }
        }
    }

   function SetDefaultValue_BillToContact() {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        var controlName = placeHolder + "SystemIndividualParticipantCombobox_35";
        var combo = $find(controlName);
            combo.clearSelection();
            combo.clearItems();
            combo.trackChanges();
        var comboItem = new Telerik.Web.UI.RadComboBoxItem();
            comboItem.set_value("0:0");
            comboItem.set_text("Same As Customer");
            combo.get_items().add(comboItem);
            combo.commitChanges();
            combo.get_items().getItem(0).select();
        }

    function SmartDataPrimaryMortgageSuggestionPopUp() {
        var clipID = getClipID();

        if (checkIsNull(clipID) == false) {
            var window = document.getElementById("SmartDataSuggestedMortgageCompanyWindow");
            var url = "https://servpro.ngsapps.net/EnterpriseApp/EnterpriseJob/SmartDataSuggestedMortgageCompany"
                + "?ClipID=" + clipID;
            
            document.getElementById("DivDarkBackground").style.display = "block";
            window.style.display = "block";
            window.style.top = checkIsNull("") ? "25%" : "5%" ;
            document.getElementById('SmartDataSuggestedMortgageCompanyIframe').src = url;

            document.getElementById('DivDarkBackground').onclick = function () {
                window.style.display = "none";
                document.getElementById("DivDarkBackground").style.display = "none";
            };
        }
    }

    function listener(event) {
        if (checkIsNull(event) == false) {
            const data = JSON.parse(event.data);

            if (data.senderWindow == 'SuggestedMortgageCompanyWindow') {
                closeSuggestionCompanyWindow();
                setSuggestedMortgageCompanyLogID(data.logID);

                if (checkIsNull(data.companyID) === false) {
                    showLogo("coreLogicLogo");
                    RebindCompany('SystemCompanyParticipantCombobox_14', data.companyID, data.companyName);
                }
            }
            else if (data.senderWindow == 'CloseSuggestedMortgageCompanyWindow') {
                closeSuggestionCompanyWindow();
                setSuggestedMortgageCompanyLogID(data.logID);
            }
        }
    }

    if (window.addEventListener) {
        addEventListener("message", listener, false)
    }
    else {
        attachEvent("onmessage", listener)
    }

    function checkIsNull(value) {
        if (value === null || value === undefined || value.length == 0) {
            return true;
        }

        return false;
    }

    function closeSuggestionCompanyWindow() {
        document.getElementById("SmartDataSuggestedMortgageCompanyWindow").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("DivDarkBackground").style.display = "none";
    }

    function enableSmartDataCompanySuggestionButton(value) {
        var suggestionButton = document.getElementById("smartDataCompanySuggestionButton");

        if (value) {
            suggestionButton.classList.add("enabledbutton");
            suggestionButton.classList.remove("disabledbutton");
        }
        else {
            suggestionButton.classList.add("disabledbutton");
            suggestionButton.classList.remove("enabledbutton");
        }
    }

    function manageCoreLogicLogo(companyID) {
        NextGear.Dash.Services.Shared.CreateClaim.DropDownsService.GetSmartDataCompanyCode(companyID, setVisiblityCoreLogicLogo);
    }

    function setVisiblityCoreLogicLogo(smartDataCompanyCode) {
        if (checkIsNull(smartDataCompanyCode)) {
            hideLogo("coreLogicLogo");
        }
        else {
            showLogo("coreLogicLogo");
        }
    }

    function setSuggestedMortgageCompanyLogID(logID) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        document.getElementById(placeHolder + "SmartDataCompanyLogID").value =
            checkIsNull(logID) ? '' : logID;
    }

    function showLogo(controlID) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        document.getElementById(placeHolder + controlID).style.display = "inline-flex";
    }

    function hideLogo(controlID) {
        var placeHolder = "ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_JobParentInformation_ExternalParticipants_";
        document.getElementById(placeHolder + controlID).style.display = "none";
    }
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        

        function GetRadWindow() {
            var oWindow = null;
            if (window.radWindow) oWindow = window.radWindow;
            else if (window.frameElement && window.frameElement.radWindow) oWindow = window.frameElement.radWindow;
            return oWindow;
        }

        function closeDialog() {
            var wnd = GetRadWindow();
            wnd.close();
        }

        function ClosePanel() {
            $find("ctl00_ctl44_QuickMenuSlidingZone").collapsePane("ctl00_ctl44_QuickMenuSlidingPane")
            var slidingPane = $('div[id$=QuickMenuSlidingPane]');
            document.getElementById(slidingPane[6].id).style.display = 'block';
        }

        function HideAddNewIcon() {
             var slidingPane = $('div[id$=QuickMenuSlidingPane]');
            document.getElementById(slidingPane[6].id).style.display = 'None';
        }

    </script>
